tu śriyā saha tad madhye ca abhavat brahmā veda vedāṅga bhūṣaṇaḥ asṛjat kṣatriyān bāhvoḥ vaiśyān tu ūrutaḥ asṛjat śūdrāḥ tu pādataḥ sṛṣṭāḥ teṣām ca eva anupūrvaśas dharma śāstram ca maryādām provāca kamalodbhavaḥ tadvat sarvam pravakṣyāmi śṛṇuta dvijasattamāḥ brāhmaṇyām brāhmaṇena eva ca utpannaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ kṛṣṇa sāraḥ mṛgaḥ yatra svabhāvāt tu pravartate ṣaṭkarmāṇi ca yāni āhuḥ brāhmaṇasya manīṣiṇaḥ adhyayana adhyāpanam ca yajanam yājanam tathā śuśrūṣā kāraṇam ca eva trividham parikīrtitam yogyān adhyāpayet śiṣyān yājyān api ca yājayet vedam eva abhyaset nityam śubhe deśe samāhitaḥ guru śuśrūṣaṇam ca eva yathānyāyam atandritaḥ sāyam prātar upāsīta vidhinā agnim dvijottamaḥ atithim ca āgatam bhaktyā pūjayet śaktitaḥ gṛhī anyān atha āgatān dṛṣṭvā pūjayet avirodhataḥ priyām hitām vadet vācam para loka avirodhinīm evam dharmaḥ samuddiṣṭaḥ brāhmaṇasya samāsatas iti śrī narasiṃhapurāṇe brāhmaṇadharmakathanam nāma saptapañcāśaḥ adhyāyaḥ SNM hārītaḥ uvāca kṣatra ādīnām pravakṣyāmi yathāvat anupūrvaśas rājya sthaḥ kṣatriyaḥ ca eva prajāḥ dharmeṇa pālayet nīti śāstra artha kuśalaḥ saṃdhi vigraha tattva vid deva brāhmaṇa bhaktaḥ ca pitṛ kārya paraḥ tathā gorakṣā kṛṣi vāṇijyam kuryāt vaiśyaḥ yathāvidhi dāna dharmam yathāśaktyā guru śuśrūṣaṇam tathā pitṛ kāryam ca tad kāle narasiṃha arcanam tathā etat āsevamānaḥ tu sa svargī syāt na saṃśayaḥ varṇa trayasya śuśrūṣām kuryāt śūdraḥ prayatnataḥ dāsa vat brāhmaṇānām ca viśeṣeṇa samācaret a yācitam pradātavyam kṛṣim vṛtti artham ācaret grahāṇām māsikam kāryam pūjanam nyāya dharmataḥ dhāraṇam jīrṇa vastrasya viprasya ucchiṣṭa mārjanam sva dāreṣu ratim kuryāt para dāra vivarjitaḥ purāṇa śravaṇam viprāt narasiṃhasya pūjanam tathā vipra namaskāram kāryam śraddhā samanvitam satya saṃbhāṣaṇam ca eva rāga dveṣa vivarjanam ittham kurvan sadā śūdraḥ manaḥ vāc kāya karmabhiḥ sthānam aindram avāpnoti naṣṭa pāpaḥ tu puṇya bhāj varṇeṣu dharmāḥ vividhāḥ mayā uktāḥ yathākramam brāhmaṇa varya sādhitāḥ śṛṇudhvam atra āśrama dharmam ādyam mayā ucyamānam kramaśas muni indrāḥ hārītaḥ uvāca guroḥ priya hitam kāryam karmaṇā manasā girā kuryāt adhyayanam pūrvam brahmacārī yathāvidhi vidhim hitvā prakurvāṇaḥ na svādhyāya phalam labhet śauca ācāram aśeṣam tu śikṣayet guru saṃnidhau ajinam daṇḍa kāṣṭham ca mekhalām ca upavītakam sāyam prātar caret bhaikṣam bhojanam saṃyata indriyaḥ alābhe tu anya gehānām pūrva purvam ca varjayet ācamya prayataḥ nityam aśnīyāt guru anujñayā snāne kṛte gurau paścāt snānam kurvīta yatnavān nṛtya gīta kathā ālāpam maithunam ca viśeṣataḥ varjayet madhu māṃsam ca rasa āsvādam tathā striyaḥ kāmam krodham ca lobham ca parivādam tathā nṛṇām strīṇām ca prekṣaṇa ālambham upaghātam parasya ca svapne siktvā brahmacārī dvijaḥ śukram akāmataḥ snātvā arkam arcayitvā agnim punar mām iti ṛcam japet āstikaḥ ahar ahar saṃdhyām tri kālam saṃyata indriyaḥ upāsīta yathānyāyam brahmacāri vrate sthitaḥ abhivādya guroḥ pādau saṃdhyā karma avasānataḥ eteṣu triṣu tuṣṭeṣu tuṣṭāḥ syuḥ sarva devatāḥ tat eṣām śāsane tiṣṭhet brahmacārī vimatsaraḥ gurave dakṣiṇām dattvā tadā sva sva icchayā vaset tena bhūyaḥ prajāyeta brahmacārī dṛḍha vrataḥ saṃprāpya vidyām api durlabhām tām phalam hi tasyāḥ sakalam hi vindati hārītaḥ uvāca gṛhīta veda adhyayanaḥ śruti śāstra artha tattva vid asamāna nāma gotrām kanyām bhrātṛ yutām śubhām sarva avayava saṃyuktām sat vṛttām udvahet tatas na udvahet kapilām kanyām na adhika aṅgīm na rogiṇīm vācālām atilomām ca na vyaṅgām bhīma darśanām na ṛkṣa vṛkṣa nadī nāmnīm na anta parvata nāmikām na pakṣi ahi preṣya nāmnīm na ca bhīṣaṇa nāmikām avyaṅga aṅgīm saumya nāmnīm haṃsa vāraṇa gāminīm tanu oṣṭha keśa daśanām mṛdu aṅgīm udvahet striyam yathāyogam tathā hi evam vivāham varṇa dharmataḥ uṣaḥ kāle samutthāya kṛta śaucaḥ dvijottamaḥ tasmāt śuṣkam atha ārdram vā bhakṣayet dantadhāvanam khadiram ca kadambam ca karañjam ca vaṭam tathā apāmārgam ca bilvam ca arkaḥ ca udumbaraḥ tathā ete praśastāḥ kathitāḥ danta dhāvana karmaṇi dantadhāvana kāṣṭham ca vakṣyāmi tad praśasta tām sarve kaṇṭakinaḥ puṇyāḥ kṣīriṇaḥ tu yaśasvinaḥ aṣṭa aṅgulena mānena tat pramāṇam iha ucyate prādeśa mātram athavā tena dantān viśodhayet pratipad darśa ṣaṣṭhīṣu navamyām ca eva sattamāḥ dantānām kāṣṭha saṃyogāt dahati āsaptamam kulam apām dvādaśa gaṇḍūṣaiḥ mukha śuddhiḥ vidhīyate mantravān prokṣya ca ātmānam prakṣipet udaka añjalim ādityena saha prātar mandehāḥ nāma rākṣasāḥ udaka añjali vikṣepaḥ gāyatryā ca abhimantritaḥ tān hanti rākṣasān sarvān mandehān ravi vairiṇaḥ tatas prayāti savitā brāhmaṇaiḥ rakṣitaḥ divi marīci ādyaiḥ mahābhāgaiḥ sanaka ādyaiḥ ca yogibhiḥ tasmāt na laṅghayet saṃdhyām sāyam prātar dvijaḥ sadā sāyam mantravat ācamya prokṣya sūryasya ca añjalim dattvā pradakṣiṇam kṛtvā jalam spṛṣṭvā viśudhyati pūrvām saṃdhyām sa nakṣatrām upakramya yathāvidhi gāyatrīm abhyaset tāvat yāvat ṛkṣāṇi paśyati tatas tu āvasatham prāpya homam kuryāt svayam budhaḥ saṃcintya bhṛtya vargasya bharaṇa artham vicakṣaṇaḥ tatas śiṣya hita arthāya svādhyāyam kiṃcid ācaret kuśa puṣpa indhana ādīni gatvā dūrāt samāharet mādhyāhnikīm kriyām kuryāt śucau deśe samāhitaḥ vidhim snānasya vakṣyāmi samāsāt pāpa nāśanam sudhīḥ snāna artham ādāya suklām kuśa tilaiḥ saha sumanāḥ ca tatas gacchet nadīm śuddhām manoramām nadyām tu vidyamānāyām na snāyāt alpa vāriṣu śucau deśe samabhyukṣya sthāpayet kuśa mṛttikām snānāt śarīram saṃśodhya kuryāt ācamanam budhaḥ tatas snānam samāsādya apaḥ ācamya mantrataḥ prokṣayet varuṇam devam taiḥ mantraiḥ pāvamānibhiḥ kuśa agra sthena toyena prokṣya ātmānam prayatnataḥ ālabhet mṛttikām gātre idam viṣṇuḥ iti tridhā tatas nārāyaṇam devam saṃsmaran praviśet jalam snātvā kuśa tilaiḥ tadvat devarṣīn pitṛbhiḥ saha jala tīram samāsādya dhaute śukle ca vāsasī paridhāya uttarīyam ca na kuryāt keśa dhūnanam na raktam ulbaṇam vāsaḥ na nīlam tat praśasyate mala aktam tu daśa ahīnam varjayet ambaram budhaḥ tatas prakṣālayet pādau mṛd toyena vicakṣaṇaḥ tris pibet vīkṣitam toyam āsyam dvis parimārjayet pādau śirasi ca abhyukṣet tris ācamya tu saṃspṛśet aṅguṣṭhena pradeśinyāḥ nāsikām samupaspṛśet aṅguṣṭha kaniṣṭhikābhyām nābhau hṛdi talena ca śiraḥ ca aṅgulibhiḥ sarvaiḥ bāhum ca eva tatas spṛśet anena vidhinā ācamya brāhmaṇaḥ śuddha mānasaḥ darbhe tu darbha pāṇiḥ syāt prāc mukhaḥ su samāhitaḥ prāṇāyāmān tu kurvīta yathāśāstram atandritaḥ japa yajñam tatas kuryāt gāyatrīm vedamātaram vācikaḥ ca upāṃśuḥ ca mānasaḥ trividhaḥ smṛtaḥ trayāṇām japa yajñānām śreyaḥ syāt uttarottamam yat ucca nīca svaritaiḥ spaṣṭa śabdavat akṣaraiḥ śabdam uccārayet vācā japa yajñaḥ sa vācikaḥ śanais uccārayet mantram īṣat oṣṭhau pracālayet kiṃcid mantram svayam vindyāt upāṃśuḥ sa japaḥ smṛtaḥ dhiyā yat akṣara śreṇyā varṇāt varṇam padāt padam śabda artha cintanam dhyānam tat uktam mānasam japaḥ japena devatā nityam stūyamānā prasīdati prasannā vipulān bhogān dadyāt muktim ca śāśvatīm yakṣa rakṣaḥ piśācāḥ ca grahāḥ sūrya ādi dūṣaṇāḥ ṛkṣa ādikam parijñāya japa yajñam atandritaḥ japet ahar ahar snātvā sāvitrīm tad manāḥ dvijaḥ sahasra paramām devīm śata madhyām daśa avarām atha puṣpa añjalim dattvā bhānave ca ūrdhvabāhukaḥ pradakṣiṇam upāvṛtya namaḥ kuryāt divākaram devān deva gaṇān ca eva ṛṣīn ṛṣi gaṇān tathā pitṝn pitṛ gaṇān ca eva nityam saṃtarpayet budhaḥ snāna vastram tatas pīḍya punar ācamanam caret darbheṣu darbha pāṇiḥ syāt brahmayajña vidhānataḥ utthāya mūrdha paryantam haṃsaḥ śuciṣad iti ṛcā godoha mātram atithim prativīkṣeta vai gṛhī a dṛṣṭa pūrvam atithim āgatam prāk samarcayet āgatya ca punar dvāram pratyutthānena sādhunā svāgatena agnayaḥ tuṣṭāḥ bhavanti gṛhamedhinām pāda śaucena pitaraḥ prītim āyānti tasya ca tasmāt atithaye kāryam pūjanam gṛhamedhinā bhikṣām ca bhikṣave dadyāt parivrāj brahmacāriṇe dadyāt ca manasā nityam bhikṣām bhikṣoḥ prayatnataḥ a kṛte vaiśvadeve tu bhikṣau bhikṣā artham āgate uddhṛtya vaiśvadeva annam bhikṣām dattvā visarjayet vaiśvadeva a kṛtam doṣam śaktaḥ bhikṣuḥ vyapohitum suvāsinīḥ kumārīḥ ca bhojayitvā āturān api bāla vṛddhān tatas śeṣam svayam bhuñjīta vai gṛhī prāc mukha udak mukhaḥ vā api maunī ca mita bhāṣaṇaḥ annam pūrvam namaskṛtya prahṛṣṭena antarātmanā pañca prāṇa āhutīḥ kuryāt sa mantreṇa pṛthak pṛthak tatas svādu karam ca annam bhuñjīta su samāhitaḥ ācamya devatām iṣṭām saṃsmaret udaram spṛśan itihāsa purāṇābhyām kaṃcid kālam nayet budhaḥ tatas saṃdhyām upāsīta bahis gatvā vidhānataḥ kṛta homaḥ ca bhuñjīta rātrau atithim arcayet sāyam prātar dvijātīnām aśanam śruti coditam smṛti uktān sakalān pūrvam purāṇa uktān api dvijaḥ mahānavamyām dvādaśyām bharaṇyām api ca eva hi tathā akṣayya tṛtīyāyām śiṣyān na adhyāpayet budhaḥ dānam ca vidhinā deyam gṛhasthena hita eṣiṇā hiraṇya dānam go dānam bhūmi dānam viśeṣataḥ maṅgalācāra yuktaḥ ca śuciḥ śraddhā paraḥ gṛhī śrāddham ca śraddhayā kuryāt sa yāti brahmaṇaḥ padam jātau utkarṣam āyāti narasiṃha prasādataḥ sa tasmāt muktim āpnoti brahmaṇā saha sattamāḥ evam hi viprāḥ kathitaḥ mayā vaḥ samāsatas śāśvata dharma rāśiḥ iti śrī narasiṃhapurāṇe gṛhasthadharmaḥ nāma aṣṭapañcāśaḥ adhyāyaḥ SNM hārītaḥ uvāca atas param pravakṣyāmi vānaprasthasya lakṣaṇam dharmam agryam mahābhāgāḥ kathyamānam nibodhata gṛhasthaḥ putra pautra ādīn dṛṣṭvā palitam ātmanaḥ sva bhāryām tanaye sthāpye sva śiṣyaiḥ praviśet vanam jaṭā kalāpa cīrāṇi nakha gātra ruhāṇi vā bhṛta parṇaiḥ mṛd saṃbhūtaiḥ nīvāra ādyaiḥ atandritaḥ tri kālam snāna yuktaḥ tu kuryāt tīvram tapaḥ sadā pakṣe gate vā aśnīyāt māsa ante vā parāka kṛt catuṣkāle api ca aśnīyāt kāle api uta tathā aṣṭame ṣaṣṭhāhna kāle hi athavā athavā vāyubhakṣakaḥ agnim ca ātmani vai kṛtvā vrajet vā atha uttarām diśam ā dehapātāt vana gaḥ maunam āsthāya tāpasaḥ vimukta pāpaḥ hi manaḥ praśāntaḥ prayāti viṣṇoḥ sadanam dvijendraḥ iti śrī narasiṃhapurāṇe vānaprasthadharmaḥ nāma ekonaṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ SNM hārītaḥ uvāca evam vana āśrame tiṣṭhan tapasā dagdha kilbiṣaḥ divyam ṛṣibhyaḥ devebhyaḥ sva pitṛbhyaḥ ca yatnataḥ dattvā śrāddham ṛṣibhyaḥ ca manujebhyaḥ tathā ātmane iṣṭim vaiśvānarīm kṛtvā prājāpatyam atha api vā dadyāt ca bhūmau udakam sarva bhūta abhayaṃkaram tri daṇḍam vaiṇavam saumyam sa tvacam sama parvakam veṣṭitam kṛṣṇa go vāla rajjvā ca catur aṅgulam gṛhṇīyāt dakṣiṇe haste mantreṇa eva tu mantra vid kaupīnāt chādanam vāsaḥ kuthām śīta nivāriṇīm pāduke ca api gṛhṇīyāt kuryāt na anyasya saṃgraham etāni tasya liṅgāni yateḥ proktāni dharmataḥ saṃgṛhya kṛta saṃnyāsaḥ gatvā tīrtham anuttamam āsīnaḥ prāc mukhaḥ maunī prāṇāyāma trayam caret gāyatrīm ca yathāśakti japtvā dhyāyet param padam sāyāhna kāle viprāṇām gṛhāṇi vicaret yatiḥ syāt arthī yāvatā annena tāvat bhaikṣam samācaret sūrya ādi daivatebhyaḥ hi dattvā annam prokṣya vāriṇā bhuñjīta parṇapuṭake pātre vā vagyataḥ yatiḥ kovidāra karañjeṣu na bhūñjīta kadācana japa dhyāna itihāsaiḥ tu dina śeṣam nayet yatiḥ palāśāḥ sarve ucyante yatayaḥ kāṃsya bhojinaḥ kāṃsya bhojī yatiḥ sarvam prāpnuyāt kilbiṣam punar na duṣyet tasya tat pātram yajñeṣu camasāḥ iva kṛta saṃdhyaḥ tatas rātrim nayet devagṛha ādiṣu hṛd puṇḍarīka nilaye dhyāyan nārāyaṇam harim iti śrī narasiṃhapurāṇe yatidharmaḥ nāma ṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ SNM hārītaḥ uvāca varṇānām āśramāṇām ca kathitam dharma lakṣaṇam yoga śāstrasya vakṣyāmi saṃkṣepāt sāram uttamam yasya abhyāsa balāt yānti mokṣam ca iha mumukṣavaḥ yoga abhyāsa ratasya iha naśyeyuḥ pātakāni ca prāṇāyāmena vacanam pratyāhāreṇa ca indriyam dhāraṇābhiḥ vaśīkṛtya punar durdharṣaṇam manaḥ ekam kāraṇam ānanda bodham ca tam anāmayam sukṣmāt sūkṣmataram dhyāyet jagat ādhāram acyutam rahasi ekāntam āsīta dhyāyet ātma hṛdi sthitam yaḥ sarva prāṇa citta jñaḥ yaḥ sarveṣām hṛdi sthitaḥ ātma lābha sukham yāvat tāvat dhyānam udāhṛtam yathā aśvāḥ ratha hīnāḥ ca rathāḥ ca aśvaiḥ vinā yathā evam tapaḥ ca vidyā ca saṃyukte bheṣajam mahat dvābhyām eva hi pakṣābhyām yathā vai pakṣiṇām gatiḥ tathā eva jñāna karmabhyām prāpyate brahma śāśvatam vidyā tapobhyām saṃpannaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ yoga tatparaḥ na deva yāna mārgeṇa yāvat prāptam param padam mayā vaḥ kathitaḥ sarvaḥ varṇa āśrama vibhāgaśaḥ saṃkṣepeṇa dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ dharmaḥ teṣām sanātanaḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ uvāca praṇamya tam ṛṣim jagmuḥ muditāḥ te svam ālayam dharma śāstram idam yaḥ tu hārīta mukha niḥsṛtam śrutvā ca kurute dharmam sa yāti paramām gatim svam svam karma prakurvāṇāḥ vipra ādyāḥ yānti sat gatim yasya ye abhihitāḥ dharmāḥ sa tu taiḥ taiḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ catur varṇāḥ ca rāja indra catvāraḥ ca api ca āśramāḥ svadharmeṇa yathā nṛṇām narasiṃhaḥ pratuṣyati varṇa dharma anusāreṇa narasiṃham tathā arcayet satya ātmakam cit sukha rūpam ādyam vihāya deham padam eti viṣṇoḥ iti śrī narasiṃhapurāṇe yogādhyāyaḥ nāma ekaṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ SNM śrī mārkaṇḍeyaḥ uvāca varṇānām āśramāṇām ca kathitam lakṣaṇam tava bhūyas kathaya rāja indra śuśrūṣā tatra kā nṛpa sahasrānīkaḥ uvāca tāni sthānāni tān mantrān tvam ācakṣva mahā mune śrī mārkaṇḍeyaḥ uvāca arcanam saṃpravakṣyāmi viṣṇoḥ amita tejasaḥ yat kṛtvā munayaḥ sarve param nirvāṇam āpnuyuḥ agnau kriyāvatām devaḥ hṛdi devaḥ manīṣiṇām pratimāsu alpabuddhīnām yoginām hṛdaye hariḥ ānuṣṭubhasya sūktasya viṣṇuḥ tasya ca devatā puruṣaḥ yaḥ jagat bījam ṛṣiḥ nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ dadyāt puruṣasūktena yaḥ puṣpāṇi apaḥ eva ca ādyayā āvāhayet devam ṛcā tu puruṣottamam dvitīyayā āsanam dadyāt pādyam dadyāt tṛtīyayā caturthyā arghyaḥ pradātavyaḥ pañcamyā ācamanīyakam ṣaṣṭhyā snānam prakurvīta saptamyā vastram eva ca yajñopavītam aṣṭamyāḥ navamyāḥ gandham eva ca daśamyā puṣpa dānam syāt ekādaśyā ca dhūpakam dvādaśyā ca tathā dīpam trayodaśyā arcanam tathā caturdaśyā stutim kṛtvā pañcadaśyā pradakṣiṇam ṣoḍaśyā udvāsanam kuryāt śeṣa karmāṇi pūrvavat snānam vastram ca naivedyam dadyāt ācanamīyakam ṣaṣ māsāt siddhim āpnoti devadevam samarcayan śaṅkha cakra gadā pāṇim dhyātvā viṣṇum upāsate dhyeyaḥ sadā savitṛ maṇḍala madhya vartī nārāyaṇaḥ sarasija āsana saṃniviṣṭaḥ keyūravān makara kuṇḍalavān kirīṭī hārī hiraṇmaya vapuḥ dhṛta śaṅkha cakraḥ sa sarva pāpam pravihāya vaiṣṇavam padam prayāti acyuta tuṣṭi kṛt naraḥ anena nityam kuru viṣṇu pūjām prāptum tat iṣṭam yadi vaiṣṇavam padam iti śrī narasiṃhapurāṇe viṣṇorarcāvidhiḥ nāma dviṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ SNM sahasrānīkaḥ uvāca viṣṇoḥ devātidevasya pūjanam prati me adhunā śrī mārkaṇḍeyaḥ uvāca aṣṭa akṣareṇa deveśam narasiṃham anāmayam rājan aṣṭa akṣaraḥ mantraḥ sarva pāpa haraḥ paraḥ samasta yajña phala daḥ sarva śānti karaḥ śubhaḥ om namaḥ nārāyaṇāya anena abhyarcitaḥ devaḥ prītaḥ bhavati tad kṣaṇāt om namaḥ nārāyaṇāya iti mantraḥ sarva artha sādhakaḥ imam mantram japet yaḥ tu śuciḥ bhūtvā samāhitaḥ sarva pāpa vinirmuktaḥ viṣṇu sāyujyam āpnuyāt tasmāt kuru nṛpa śreṣṭha pratimā ādiṣu ca arcanam dānāni vipra mukhebhyaḥ prayaccha vidhinā nṛpa vairāgyasya api jananam saṃbhūtam bāhya vastuṣu dhruvam virāgīkṛta mānasānām svargasya rājyam na ca kiṃcid eva maitrī ādi saṃyoga parāṅmukhānām vimukti bhājām na tapaḥ na bhogaḥ vimṛśya ca etat sa sura adhināthaḥ vimānam āruhya sa kiṅkiṇīkam nūnam hara ārādhana kāraṇena kailāsam abhyeti vimukti kāmaḥ saḥ ekadā mānasam āgataḥ san saṃvīkṣya tām yakṣapateḥ ca kāntām samarcayantīm girijā aṅghri yugmam dhvajām iva anaṅga mahā rathasya pradhāna jāmbūnada śuddha varṇām karṇa anta saṃlagna manojña netrām su sūkṣma vastra antara dṛśya gātrām nīhāra madhyāt iva candralekhām tām vīkṣya vīkṣaṇa aṅga śarīra rūpam mokṣaḥ amunā yadi api mohanīyaḥ mokṣe api kim kāraṇam asti rājye kṣetram su pakvam parihṛtya dvāre kim nāma ca araṇya kṛṣim karoti saṃsāra duḥkha upahatāḥ narāḥ ye kartum samarthāḥ na ca kiṃcid eva akarmiṇaḥ bhāgya vivarjitāḥ ca vāñchanti te mokṣa patham vimūḍhāḥ etat vimṛśya bahudhā matimān pravīraḥ rūpeṇa mohita manāḥ dhanada aṅganāyāḥ purā maheśena kṛta aṅga nāśaḥ dhairyāt manogatam tat paramam tutoṣa etām anaṅga āyata locana ākhyām mad aṅga saṅga ekarasām vidhehi saṃdhāya bāṇam kusumāyudhaḥ api sasmāra māraḥ parimohanam sudhīḥ saṃmohitā puṣpa śareṇa bālā kāmena kāmam mada vihvala aṅgī vihāya pūjām hasate sureśam kaḥ kāma kodaṇḍa ravam saheta saṃmohayanti iva manāṃsi puṃsām kasya iha kāntāḥ vada puṇya bhājaḥ uktā api bālā mada vihvala aṅgī romāñca saṃsveda sa kampa gātrā kṛta ākulā kāma śilīmukhena sa gadgadam vākyam uvāca mandam kāntā dhaneśasya ca yakṣa kanyā prāptā ca gaurī caraṇa arcanāya prabrūhi kāryam ca tava asti nātha kaḥ tvam vadeḥ tiṣṭhasi kāmarūpaḥ sā tvam samāgaccha bhajasva mām cirāt mad aṅga saṅga utsuka tām vraja āśu tvayā vinā jīvitam api analpam svargasya rājyam mama niṣphalam syāt vimānam āruhya calat patākam sureśa kaṇṭha grahaṇam cakāra āgatāḥ yakṣapateḥ samīpam nāryaḥ anuvarjya eva ca citrasenām sa saṃbhramāḥ saṃbhrama khinna gātrāḥ sa gadgadam procuḥ asāhasajñāḥ nūnam samākarṇaya yakṣa nātha vimānam āropya jagāma kaścid saṃvīkṣamāṇaḥ kakubhaḥ api kāntām vigṛhya vegāt iha saḥ api taskaraḥ vacaḥ niśamya atha dhanādhināthaḥ viṣa upamam jāta maṣī nibha ānanaḥ jagāda bhūyas na ca kiṃcid eva babhūva vai vṛkṣaḥ iva agni dagdhaḥ vijñāpita arthaḥ vara kanyakābhiḥ yaḥ citrasenā sahacāriṇībhiḥ moha apanodāya matim dadhānaḥ sa kaṇṭha kubjaḥ api samājagāma śrutvā āgatam vīkṣya sa rājarājaḥ unmīlita akṣaḥ vacanam jagāda viniḥśvasan gāḍha sa kampa gātraḥ svastham manaḥ api āśu vidhāya dīnaḥ dhik me dhanam jīvitam ati analpam rājyam bṛhat saṃprati guhyakānām viśāmi ca agnim na ca veda kaścid parābhavaḥ asti iti ca kaḥ mṛtānām pārśve sthitasya api ca jīvitaḥ me gatā taḍāgam girijā arcanāya hṛtā ca kena api vayam na vidmaḥ dhruvam na tasya asti bhayam ca mṛtyoḥ jagāda vākyam sa ca kaṇṭha kubjaḥ moha apanodāya vibhoḥ sa mantrī ākarṇyatām nātha na ca asti yogyaḥ kāntā viyoge nija deha ghātaḥ ekā purā rāma vadhūḥ hṛtā ca niśācareṇa api mṛtaḥ na saḥ api anekaśas santi tava atra nāryaḥ kaḥ nāma citte kriyate viṣādaḥ bhṛśam na jalpanti rudanti sādhavaḥ parābhavam bāhya kṛtam sahante sahāya kāryam kurute hi saṃprati svayam hi yasya avarajaḥ vibhīṣaṇaḥ vibhīṣaṇaḥ me pratipakṣa bhūtaḥ dāyāda bhāvam na vimuñcati iti dhruvam prasannāḥ na bhavanti durjanāḥ kṛta upakārāḥ hari vajra niṣṭhurāḥ na ca upakāraiḥ na guṇaiḥ na sauhṛdaiḥ prasādam āyāti manaḥ hi gotriṇaḥ uvāca vākyam sa ca kaṇṭha kubjaḥ yuktam tvayā uktam ca dhanādhinātha parābhavam na anya kṛtam sahante na uṣṇam jalam jvālayate tṛṇāni tasmāt samāgaccha dhanādhinātha pārśvam na vegena vibhīṣaṇasya iti uktaḥ sa tadā tena kaṇṭha kubjena mantriṇā mayā aham svāmī surāṇām ca śāpam mā dehi me adhunā nūnam tapaḥ vane asmākam duṣṭāḥ tiṣṭhanti sādhavaḥ iti uktaḥ hi tadā ca indraḥ prāptaḥ strī tvam na saṃśayaḥ jagāma tridivam bhūpa hata śakti samanvitāḥ kāntā dhanādhināthasya gūḍhā tiṣṭhati yā vibho tām ca tasmai pradāsyāmaḥ sarve kṛtvā parām matim trayodaśyām caturdaśyām devarājaḥ śacī yutaḥ nandane ca arcanam kartā sarvadā yakṣa rakṣasām ślokam śloka ardham eva vā na teṣām pāpa bandhaḥ tu kadācid api jāyate viṣṇu arpitam idam puṇyam purāṇam sarva kāma dam bhaktyā ca vadatām etat śṛṇvatām ca phalam śṛṇu śata janma arjitaiḥ pāpaiḥ sadyas eva vimocitāḥ yaḥ paṭhet prātar utthāya yat asya śloka viṃśatim jyotiṣṭoma phalam prāpya viṣṇu loke mahīyate etat pavitram pūjyam ca na vācyam akṛtātmanām dvijānām viṣṇu bhaktānām śrāvyam etat na saṃśayaḥ vadatām śṛṇvatām sadyas sarva pāpa praṇāśanam bahunā atra kim uktena bhūyas bhūyas muni īśvarāḥ bhāradvāja mukhāḥ sarve kṛtakṛtyāḥ dvijottamāḥ sūtam hṛṣṭāḥ prapūjya atha sarve sva sva āśramam yayuḥ iti śrī narasiṃhapurāṇe sūta bharadvāja ādi saṃvāde sarva duḥkha upaharam śrī narasiṃhapurāṇasya māhātmyam samāp SNPaNe
